  28 #	General notes:
  29 #
  30 #	This table contains the data the Unicode Consortium has on how
  31 #       JIS X 0212 (1983) characters map into Unicode.
  32 #
  33 #	Format:  Three tab-separated columns
  34 #		 Column #1 is the JIS X 0212 code (in hex as 0xXXXX)
  35 #		 Column #2 is the Unicode (in hex as 0xXXXX)
  36 #		 Column #3 the Unicode name (follows a comment sign, '#')
  37 #					The official names for Unicode characters U+4E00
  38 #					to U+9FA5, inclusive, is "CJK UNIFIED IDEOGRAPH-XXXX",
  39 #					where XXXX is the code point.  Including all these
  40 #					names in this file increases its size substantially
  41 #					and needlessly.  The token "<CJK>" is used for the
  42 #					name of these characters.  If necessary, it can be
  43 #					expanded algorithmically by a parser or editor.
  44 #
  45 #	The entries are in JIS X 0212 order
  46 #
  47 #	The following algorithms can be used to change the hex form
  48 #		of JIS 0212 to other standard forms:
  49 #
  50 #		To change hex to EUC form, add 0x8080
  51 #		To change hex to kuten form, first subtract 0x2020.  Then
  52 #			the high and low bytes correspond to the ku and ten of
  53 #			the kuten form.  For example, 0x2121 -> 0x0101 -> 0101;
  54 #			0x6D63 -> 0x4D43 -> 7767
  55 #
  56 #   The kanji mappings are a normative part of ISO/IEC 10646.  The
  57 #       non-kanji mappings are provisional, pending definition of
  58 #       official mappings by Japanese standards bodies
  59 #
  60 #	Any comments or problems, contact <John_Jenkins@taligent.com>
  61 #
  62 #	Notes:
  63 #
  64 #	1. JIS X 0212 apparently unified the following two symbols
  65 #	   into a single character at 0x2922:
  66 #	
  67 #	   LATIN CAPITAL LETTER D WITH STROKE
  68 #	   LATIN CAPITAL LETTER ETH
  69 #
  70 #	   However, JIS X 0212 maintains the distinction between
  71 #	   the lowercase forms of these two elements at 0x2942 and 0x2943.
  72 #	   Given the structre of these JIS encodings, it is clear that
  73 #	   0x2922 and 0x2942 are intended to be a capital/small pair.
  74 #	   Consequently, in the Unicode mapping, 0x2922 is treated as
  75 #	   LATIN CAPITAL LETTER D WITH STROKE.
  76 #
